	{
		var ck = document.cookie;
        var exp1 = new RegExp(name + "=.*?(?=;|$)");
        var mch = ck.match(exp1);
        return  mch ? unescape(mch[0].substring(name.length + 1)) : null;
	}

      function NavLableStat()
    {
        var li = $(".car-list-details").children();

        //热门标签
        var heatLabel = li.eq(0);
        var leftBtn = heatLabel.find(".arrow-left-lg.focus-button.focus-left");
        var rightBtn = heatLabel.find(".arrow-right-lg.focus-button.focus-right");
        leftBtn.eq(0).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2249");
        leftBtn.eq(1).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2247");
        leftBtn.eq(2).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2245");
        rightBtn.eq(0).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2249");
        rightBtn.eq(1).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2247");
        rightBtn.eq(2).attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2245");
        var content = heatLabel.find(".slide-box-big");
        content.eq(0).find("a").attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2248");
        content.eq(1).find("a").attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2246");
        content.eq(2).find("a").attr("data-channelid", "1.61.2244");
        //豪华车
        var lisub1 = li.eq(2);
        AddAttribute(lisub1, "1.61.2259");
        //0-8万
        var lisub1 = li.eq(3);
        AddAttribute(lisub1, "1.61.2250");
        //8-12万
        var lisub2 = li.eq(4);
        AddAttribute(lisub2, "1.61.2251");
        //12-18万
        var lisub3 = li.eq(5);
        AddAttribute(lisub3, "1.61.2252");
        //18-25万
        var lisub4 = li.eq(6);
        AddAttribute(lisub4, "1.61.2253");
        //25-40万
        var lisub5 = li.eq(7);
        AddAttribute(lisub5, "1.61.2254");
        //40-80万
        var lisub6 = li.eq(8);
        AddAttribute(lisub6, "1.61.2255");
        //80万以上
        var lisub7 = li.eq(9);
        AddAttribute(lisub7, "1.61.2256");
    }
    function AddAttribute(li, value) {
        var leftBtn = $(li).find(".focus-left");
        var rightBtn = $(li).find(".focus-right");
        if (leftBtn.length > 0) {
            leftBtn.attr("data-channelid", value);
        }

        if (rightBtn.length > 0) {
            rightBtn.attr("data-channelid", value);
        }
    }
